\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00157}00157\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ We\ support\ two\ kinds\ of\ shared\ objects\ (.so):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00158}00158\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ 1)\ shared\_library,\ which\ is\ just\ bundling\ together\ many\ dependent\ libraries}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00159}00159\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ into\ a\ link\ line.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00160}00160\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ 2)\ loadable\_module,\ which\ is\ generating\ a\ module\ intended\ for\ dlopen().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00161}00161\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00162}00162\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ They\ differ\ only\ slightly:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00163}00163\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ In\ the\ former\ case,\ we\ want\ to\ package\ all\ dependent\ code\ into\ the\ .so.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00164}00164\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ In\ the\ latter\ case,\ we\ want\ to\ package\ just\ the\ API\ exposed\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00165}00165\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ outermost\ module.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00166}00166\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ This\ means\ shared\_library\ uses\ -\/-\/whole-\/archive,\ while\ loadable\_module\ doesn't.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{make_8py_source_l00167}00167\ \textcolor{stringliteral}{\#\ (Note\ that\ -\/-\/whole-\/archive\ is\ incompatible\ with\ the\ -\/-\/start-\/group\ used\ in}}
